      <foreign lang="ar">فى <ref cref="n6415-30" target="جَانِبِه" n="30" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, i. e. <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">O my grief,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">regret, for my negligence,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">remissness,</hi>] <hi rend="ital">in respect of that which is the right,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">due, of God!</hi> (A, Bd, TA,) i. e., (Bd,) <hi rend="ital">in respect of obedience to God!</hi> (Bd, Jel:) or, <hi rend="ital">in respect of</hi> [<hi rend="ital">the means of attaining</hi>] <hi rend="ital">nearness to God!</hi> (Fr, TA;) or, <hi rend="ital">nearness to God in Paradise!</hi> (IAar, TA:) or, <hi rend="ital">in respect of the way of God, to which He hath called me!</hi> i. e., the profession of his unity, and the confession of the prophetic office of Mohammad. (Zj, TA.) The saying of the Arabs, <foreign lang="ar">اِتَّقِ ٱللّٰهَ فِى جَنْبِهِ وَلَا تَقْدَحْ فِى سَاقِهِ</foreign> [may be rendered <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">Fear God in respect of his</hi> (thy brother's) <hi rend="ital">right,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">due, and impugn not his honour,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">reputation:</hi> or] means, accord. to the copies of the K, <foreign lang="ar">لَا تَقْتُلْهُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">slay him not</hi>], or, as in the L, and in the original draught of the author [of the K] <foreign lang="ar">لا تَغْتَلْهُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">slay him not clandestinely,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">on an occasion of inadvertence</hi>], from <foreign lang="ar">الغِيلَةُ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">and throw him not into trouble,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">trial:</hi> (TA:) or, accord. to some, <foreign lang="ar">فى جنبه</foreign> means <hi rend="ital">in detracting from his reputation,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">reviling him.</hi> (K, TA.                      </L> 
                  </quote> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">O my two friends, refrain, and be mindful of God in respect of my reputation;</hi> (see also <foreign lang="ar">جَانِبٌ</foreign>;)] meaning, <hi rend="ital">in detracting from my reputation,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">reviling me:</hi> or, accord. to MF, <hi rend="ital">in my case.</hi> (TA.) (Msb.) <foreign lang="ar">الجَارُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الجُنُبُ</foreign> [occurring in the Kur iv. 40] (T, S, A, Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">جَارُ الجُنُبِ</foreign> (TA) <hi rend="ital">The person who is one's neighbour, but who belongs to another people;</hi> (T, S, A, Msb, K;) <hi rend="ital">who is not of one's family nor of one's lineage;</hi> (A;) <hi rend="ital">who is of another lineage than he of whom he is a neighbour;</hi> (T, TA;) <hi rend="ital">who is not a relation:</hi> (MF:) or <hi rend="ital">one who is distant,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">remote, in an absolute sense:</hi> (TA:) or <hi rend="ital">the person who is not a relation to another, and who comes to him, and asks him to protect him, and abides with him:</hi> such has the title to respect that belongs to him as neighbour of the other, and to his protection, and as relying upon his safeguard and promise. (TA in art. <foreign lang="ar">جور</foreign>. [Differing from <foreign lang="ar">جَارُ الجَنْبِ</foreign>, q. v. suprà.]) It is said in a trad., <foreign lang="ar">هُمْ أَجْنَابُ النَّاسِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">They are the strangers of mankind,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">of the people.</hi> (TA.)
